Method: 引入“结构=基序+晶格”（SML）的MCN结构设计新范式，将MCN设计解耦为局部基序设计和全局晶格设计。提出“高可用性低延迟巨型星座设计”（HALLMD）问题，旨在最大化ISL可用性同时最小化传输延迟。为解决HALLMD，本文提出一种启发式算法SMLOP，能在多项式时间内高效找到最优网络结构。

Result: 在四种先进的公共星座上的实验验证表明，与现有技术相比，容量提升了5%~18%，吞吐量增加了1%~12%，路径拉伸减少了12%~23%，往返时间（RTT）减少了8%~77%。

Conclusion: SML范式和SMLOP算法为巨型星座网络结构设计提供了一种高效解决方案，能够显著提高网络容量、吞吐量，并大幅降低传输延迟，从而实现高可用性和低延迟的巨型星座网络。

Abstract: The network structure design plays a vital role in the mega-constellation
network (MSN) to coordinate massive network nodes to ensure the effectiveness
and reliability of operations and services for future space wireless
communications networks.
  One of the critical issues in MCN is how to design an optimal network control
structure by configuring the most stable inter-satellite link (ISL) to achieve
high available MCN within a limited average transmission delays.
  To address this problem, this paper introduces a novel MCN structure design
paradigm: Structure = Motif + Lattice (SML), which decouples MCN design into
local motifs design and global lattices design. Specifically, we formulate the
High-Availability and Low-Latency Mega-Constellation Design (HALLMD) problem,
aimed at maximizing ISL availability while minimizing the transmission latency.
To solve HALLMD, we propose SMLOP, a heuristic algorithm that efficiently finds
optimal network structures in polynomial time. Experimental validation on four
public state-of-the-art constellations demonstrates significant improvements,
including enhanced capacity by $5\sim 18\%$, increased throughput by $1\sim
12\%$, reduced path stretch by $12\sim 23\%$, and Round-Trip Time (RTT) by

### [228] [Disentangling the Drivers of LLM Social Conformity: An Uncertainty-Moderated Dual-Process Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14918)
*Huixin Zhong,Yanan Liu,Qi Cao,Shijin Wang,Zijing Ye,Zimu Wang,Shiyao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CY

TL;DR: 研究发现大型语言模型（LLMs）的社会从众行为主要源于信息性影响，但高不确定性会引发类似规范性影响的放大效应，导致其过度权衡公开信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型（LLMs）融入协作团队，它们的社会从众行为（即与多数意见保持一致的倾向）成为一个关键问题。在人类中，从众行为源于信息性影响（理性利用群体线索以提高准确性）或规范性影响（社会压力以获得认同），且不确定性会调节这种平衡。目前尚不清楚这些人类心理机制是否适用于LLMs。本研究旨在探究LLMs的从众机制及其受不确定性调节的影响。

Method: 本研究采用了行为经济学中的“信息级联范式”，以定量方式分离信息性影响和规范性影响这两个驱动因素，并探究不确定性的调节作用。我们评估了九个主流LLMs，涉及医疗、法律和投资三种决策场景，并操纵了信息不确定性（q分别为0.667、0.55和0.70）。

Result: 结果表明，信息性影响是LLMs在所有情境下行为的基础，准确性和置信度随证据强度持续上升。然而，这一基础机制受到不确定性的显著调节。在中低不确定性情境下，这种信息处理过程表现为一种保守策略，LLMs系统性地低估所有证据来源。相反，高不确定性触发了一个关键转变：在继续处理信息的同时，模型额外表现出一种类似规范性的放大效应，导致它们过度权衡公共信号（beta > 1.55 对比私有beta = 0.81）。

Conclusion: LLMs的从众行为主要由信息性影响驱动。但在高不确定性条件下，LLMs会表现出类似规范性的行为，即过度放大公共信号。这表明不确定性是调节LLMs从众行为的关键因素，其从众行为并非纯粹的理性信息处理。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) integrate into collaborative teams, their
social conformity -- the tendency to align with majority opinions -- has
emerged as a key concern. In humans, conformity arises from informational
influence (rational use of group cues for accuracy) or normative influence
(social pressure for approval), with uncertainty moderating this balance by
shifting from purely analytical to heuristic processing. It remains unclear
whether these human psychological mechanisms apply to LLMs. This study adapts
the information cascade paradigm from behavioral economics to quantitatively
disentangle the two drivers to investigate the moderate effect. We evaluated
nine leading LLMs across three decision-making scenarios (medical, legal,
investment), manipulating information uncertainty (q = 0.667, 0.55, and 0.70,
respectively). Our results indicate that informational influence underpins the
models' behavior across all contexts, with accuracy and confidence consistently
rising with stronger evidence. However, this foundational mechanism is
dramatically modulated by uncertainty. In low-to-medium uncertainty scenarios,
this informational process is expressed as a conservative strategy, where LLMs
systematically underweight all evidence sources. In contrast, high uncertainty
triggers a critical shift: while still processing information, the models
additionally exhibit a normative-like amplification, causing them to overweight
public signals (beta > 1.55 vs. private beta = 0.81).

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Variations in complex traits are influenced by multiple genetic variants,

has been made in identifying single genetic variants associated with complex
traits, detecting the gene-gene and gene-environment interactions remains a
great challenge. When a large number of genetic variants and environmental risk
factors are involved, searching for interactions is limited to pair-wise
interactions due to the exponentially increased feature space and computational
intensity. Alternatively, recursive partitioning approaches, such as random
forests, have gained popularity in high-dimensional genetic association
studies. In this article, we propose a U-Statistic-based random forest
approach, referred to as Forest U-Test, for genetic association studies with
quantitative traits. Through simulation studies, we showed that the Forest
U-Test outperformed existing methods. The proposed method was also applied to
study Cannabis Dependence CD, using three independent datasets from the Study
of Addiction: Genetics and Environment. A significant joint association was
detected with an empirical p-value less than 0.001. The finding was also
replicated in two independent datasets with p-values of 5.93e-19 and 4.70e-17,
respectively.

### [232] [TOM: An Open-Source Tongue Segmentation Method with Multi-Teacher Distillation and Task-Specific Data Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14932)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 舌像分割质量对智能舌诊系统的分类和诊断精度至关重要。然而，现有舌像分割研究存在局限性，且缺乏鲁棒、用户友好的分割工具。

Method: 本研究提出了一种基于多教师知识蒸馏的舌像分割模型（TOM），并结合了一种新颖的基于扩散的数据增强方法，以提升模型的泛化能力并减小参数规模。此外，还将训练好的模型封装为在线和离线工具，并进行了中医体质分类的案例研究，使用分割后的舌面图像进行训练。

Result: 与教师模型相比，学生模型参数量减少了96.6%，但仍达到了95.22%的mIoU分割性能。模型被部署为在线和离线分割工具（https://itongue.cn/），方便用户使用。在基于分割舌面图像进行中医体质分类的案例研究中，展示了更高的分类性能和更好的可解释性。

Abstract: Tongue imaging serves as a valuable diagnostic tool, particularly in
Traditional Chinese Medicine (TCM). The quality of tongue surface segmentation
significantly affects the accuracy of tongue image classification and
subsequent diagnosis in intelligent tongue diagnosis systems. However, existing

lack of robust and user-friendly segmentation tools. This paper proposes a
tongue image segmentation model (TOM) based on multi-teacher knowledge
distillation. By incorporating a novel diffusion-based data augmentation
method, we enhanced the generalization ability of the segmentation model while
reducing its parameter size. Notably, after reducing the parameter count by
96.6% compared to the teacher models, the student model still achieves an
impressive segmentation performance of 95.22% mIoU. Furthermore, we packaged
and deployed the trained model as both an online and offline segmentation tool

to use it without any programming experience. We also present a case study on
TCM constitution classification using segmented tongue patches. Experimental
results demonstrate that training with tongue patches yields higher
classification performance and better interpretability than original tongue
images. To our knowledge, this is the first open-source and freely available
tongue image segmentation tool.

*Nan-Hong Kuo,Renata Wong*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究建立了SVM核函数与量子传播子（格林函数）的数学等价性，并通过数值实验证明了对应格林函数的核函数能显著提高SVM在物理系统中的预测精度，并引入了一种核多项式方法来设计定制化核函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SVM核函数与量子传播子（由时变格林函数表示）之间的数学等价性尚未被充分探索，本研究旨在揭示并利用这一未开发的联系以提升SVM模型的性能。

Method: 1. 通过算子反演理论证明常见SVM核函数与格林函数的对应关系。 2. 引入核多项式方法（KPM）来设计与格林函数对齐的定制化核函数。 3. 进行数值实验验证所提方法的有效性。

Result: 1. 许多常见SVM核函数可自然地对应于格林函数。 2. Sigmoid核函数并非总满足Mercer定理，其对应的格林函数表现可能不佳。 3. 使用与格林函数对应的半正定核函数显著提高了SVM模型在物理系统中的预测精度。

Conclusion: SVM核函数与量子格林函数之间存在数学等价性。利用这一发现，可以设计出与格林函数对齐的定制化核函数，从而显著提升SVM模型在物理系统等领域的预测性能。

Abstract: We establish a mathematical equivalence between Support Vector Machine (SVM)
kernel functions and quantum propagators represented by time-dependent Green's
functions, which has remained largely unexplored.
  We demonstrate that many common SVM kernels correspond naturally to Green's
functions via operator inversion theory. The sigmoid kernel does not always
satisfy Mercer's theorem, and therefore the corresponding Green's function may
also fail to perform optimally.
  We further introduce a Kernel Polynomial Method (KPM) for designing
customized kernels that align with Green's functions.
  Our numerical experiments confirm that employing positive-semidefinite
kernels that correspond to Green's functions significantly improves predictive
accuracy of SVM models in physical systems.

</details>


<div id='eess.AS'></div>

# eess.AS [[Back]](#toc)

### [234] [A Chinese Heart Failure Status Speech Database with Universal and Personalised Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14908)
*Yue Pan,Liwei Liu,Changxin Li,Xinyao Wang,Yili Xia,Hanyue Zhang,Ming Chu*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本研究建立了首个中文心力衰竭语音数据库，证实了中文语音在心力衰竭检测中的有效性，并提出自适应频率滤波器以分析频率重要性，同时指出个体差异是影响准确性的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语音是识别急慢性心力衰竭的经济有效且无创的数据源，但目前缺乏关于中文音节是否包含心力衰竭相关信息的研究。

Method: 构建了首个中文心力衰竭患者语音数据库，包含住院前后配对录音。采用标准“以患者为单位”和个性化“以配对为单位”的分类方法进行检测。提出了一种自适应频率滤波器（AFF）用于频率重要性分析。

Result: 研究结果证实了中文在心力衰竭检测中的有效性，其中“以配对为单位”的分类方法可作为理想的与说话人解耦的基线。统计测试和分类结果表明个体差异是导致不准确性的主要因素。提出了自适应频率滤波器（AFF）用于频率重要性分析。

Conclusion: 中文语音可有效用于心力衰竭检测。个体差异是影响检测准确性的关键。本研究发布的数据和方法为未来研究提供了重要基线。

Abstract: Speech is a cost-effective and non-intrusive data source for identifying
acute and chronic heart failure (HF). However, there is a lack of research on
whether Chinese syllables contain HF-related information, as observed in other
well-studied languages. This study presents the first Chinese speech database
of HF patients, featuring paired recordings taken before and after
hospitalisation. The findings confirm the effectiveness of the Chinese language
in HF detection using both standard 'patient-wise' and personalised 'pair-wise'
classification approaches, with the latter serving as an ideal
speaker-decoupled baseline for future research. Statistical tests and
classification results highlight individual differences as key contributors to
inaccuracy. Additionally, an adaptive frequency filter (AFF) is proposed for
frequency importance analysis. The data and demonstrations are published at
https://github.com/panyue1998/Voice_HF.

</details>


### [235] [Transsion Multilingual Speech Recognition System for MLC-SLM 2025 Challenge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14916)
*Xiaoxiao Li,An Zhu,Youhai Jiang,Fengjie Zhu*

Main category: eess.AS

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种Transsion语音团队为MLC-SLM 2025挑战赛开发的新型多语言ASR系统，该系统融合了冻结的Whisper-large-v3语音编码器、可训练适配器模块和集成LoRA的冻结Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct LLM，实现了9.83%的WER/CER，并在全球参赛者中排名第三。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为MLC-SLM 2025挑战赛Track 1开发并展示一种新颖的高性能多语言自动语音识别（ASR）系统，旨在通过结合大型预训练模型实现鲁棒的声学特征提取和优化的上下文语言解码。

Method: 该系统由三个主要组件构成：1) 基于Whisper-large-v3的冻结语音编码器，用于鲁棒的声学特征提取；2) 使用Linear-ReLU-Linear转换机制的可训练适配器模块，以有效对齐语音和文本表示；3) 集成可训练LoRA的冻结Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct大语言模型（LLM），用于优化上下文语言解码。该方法系统地结合了预训练模型与任务特定的微调。

Result: 该系统在评估集的11种语言上实现了9.83%的词错误率/字符错误率（WER/CER）。在全球参与者中排名第三。

Conclusion: 系统地结合预训练模型（如Whisper和Qwen2.5）与任务特定的微调（如适配器和LoRA）是一种开发高性能多语言ASR系统的有效策略，并在国际挑战赛中展现出强大的竞争力。

Abstract: This paper presents the architecture and performance of a novel Multilingual
Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) system developed by the Transsion Speech
Team for Track 1 of the MLC-SLM 2025 Challenge. The proposed system comprises
three key components: 1) a frozen Whisper-large-v3 based speech encoder,
leveraging large-scale pretraining to ensure robust acoustic feature
extraction; 2) a trainable adaptor module using Linear-ReLU-Linear
transformation mechanisms to effectively align speech and text representations;
and 3) a frozen Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct large language model (LLM) integrated with
trainable LoRA for optimized contextual linguistic decoding. By systematically
combining pretrained models with task specific fine-tuning, the system achieved
a word/character error rate (WER/CER) of 9.83% across 11 languages in the
evaluation set and ranked third place among global participants.

### [236] [Holo-Artisan: A Personalized Multi-User Holographic Experience for Virtual Museums on the Edge Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14956)
*Nan-Hong Kuo,Hojjat Baghban*

Main category: cs.MM

TL;DR: Holo-Artisan是一个结合真全息显示、个性化边缘智能和生成式AI的系统架构，旨在为虚拟博物馆提供沉浸式、多用户、高度个性化的互动体验，将静态展品转变为能与观众进行个人对话的动态艺术品。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将博物馆中静态的展品转化为动态的、有生命的艺术品；使每位参观者都能与艺术品进行个性化对话；开创文化遗产互动的新范式。

Method: 采用Holo-Artisan系统架构，结合本地边缘计算节点实时处理多用户的姿态、面部表情和语音数据；利用生成式AI模型驱动数字艺术品对每位观众进行独特响应；通过云辅助协作平台，使用通用场景描述在共享场景中组合互动，并利用光线追踪渲染高保真、个性化的视图，直接输出到无眼镜全息显示器。为保护用户隐私和持续提升个性化，系统集成了联邦学习，即边缘设备本地微调AI模型并仅共享模型更新进行聚合，从而实现低延迟、低带宽的同步共享体验和个体定制。

Result: 成功实现了虚拟博物馆中沉浸式的多用户体验；数字艺术品（例如立体蒙娜丽莎）能够实时对每位观众做出独特反应（如对一人微笑，与另一人进行语音问答）；通过边缘中心化方法，最大限度地减少了延迟和带宽使用，确保了同步的共享体验和个性化定制；通过联邦学习保留了用户隐私并持续改进个性化；将静态博物馆展品转变为与每位参观者进行个人对话的动态、有生命的艺术品。

Conclusion: Holo-Artisan系统开创了文化遗产互动的新范式，通过将静态博物馆展品转化为动态、能与每位参观者进行个人对话的“活”艺术品，极大地增强了参观体验。

Abstract: We present Holo-Artisan, a novel system architecture enabling immersive
multi-user experiences in virtual museums through true holographic displays and
personalized edge intelligence. In our design, local edge computing nodes
process real-time user data -- including pose, facial expression, and voice --
for multiple visitors concurrently. Generative AI models then drive digital
artworks (e.g., a volumetric Mona Lisa) to respond uniquely to each viewer. For
instance, the Mona Lisa can return a smile to one visitor while engaging in a
spoken Q\&A with another, all in real time. A cloud-assisted collaboration
platform composes these interactions in a shared scene using a universal scene
description, and employs ray tracing to render high-fidelity, personalized
views with a direct pipeline to glasses-free holographic displays. To preserve
user privacy and continuously improve personalization, we integrate federated
learning (FL) -- edge devices locally fine-tune AI models and share only model
updates for aggregation. This edge-centric approach minimizes latency and
bandwidth usage, ensuring a synchronized shared experience with individual
customization. Through Holo-Artisan, static museum exhibits are transformed
into dynamic, living artworks that engage each visitor in a personal dialogue,
heralding a new paradigm of cultural heritage interaction.

### [237] [Robust Symbolic Reasoning for Visual Narratives via Hierarchical and Semantically Normalized Knowledge Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14941)
*Yi-Chun Chen*

Main category: cs.MM

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解视觉叙事（如漫画）需要结构化表示，但现有的符号叙事图谱常存在不一致性和冗余性，导致相似事件被不同标注，限制了推理和泛化的有效性。

Method: 引入了一个针对层级叙事知识图谱的语义归一化框架。该方法基于认知叙事理解模型，利用词汇相似性和基于嵌入的聚类来整合语义相关的动作和事件，旨在减少标注噪声、对齐跨叙事层级的符号类别并保持可解释性。

Result: 在Manga109数据集上的漫画故事中进行了验证，将归一化应用于面板、事件和故事层级的图谱。初步评估表明，在动作检索、角色定位和事件总结等叙事推理任务中，语义归一化提高了连贯性和鲁棒性，同时保持了符号透明度。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，语义归一化是迈向可扩展、认知启发式的多模态叙事理解图谱模型的关键一步。

Abstract: Understanding visual narratives such as comics requires structured
representations that capture events, characters, and their relations across
multiple levels of story organization. However, symbolic narrative graphs often
suffer from inconsistency and redundancy, where similar actions or events are
labeled differently across annotations or contexts. Such variance limits the
effectiveness of reasoning and generalization.
  This paper introduces a semantic normalization framework for hierarchical
narrative knowledge graphs. Building on cognitively grounded models of
narrative comprehension, we propose methods that consolidate semantically
related actions and events using lexical similarity and embedding-based
clustering. The normalization process reduces annotation noise, aligns symbolic
categories across narrative levels, and preserves interpretability.
  We demonstrate the framework on annotated manga stories from the Manga109
dataset, applying normalization to panel-, event-, and story-level graphs.
Preliminary evaluations across narrative reasoning tasks, such as action
retrieval, character grounding, and event summarization, show that semantic
normalization improves coherence and robustness, while maintaining symbolic
transparency. These findings suggest that normalization is a key step toward
scalable, cognitively inspired graph models for multimodal narrative
understanding.

### [239] [Inference Time Debiasing Concepts in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14933)
*Lucas S. Kupssinskü,Marco N. Bochernitsan,Jordan Kopper,Otávio Parraga,Rodrigo C. Barros*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出DeCoDi，一种针对文本到图像扩散模型的去偏方法，通过在推理阶段调整扩散过程来避免偏见概念区域，从而减轻性别、种族和年龄偏见。该方法不影响图像质量，计算开销小，易于应用且普适性强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习去偏方法通常复杂且计算密集。研究旨在开发一种更简单、更易于实践者使用、且仅改变推理过程的去偏方法，以解决文本到图像生成模型中存在的各种偏见问题。

Method: DeCoDi通过修改扩散模型的推理过程来避免潜在维度中与偏见概念相关的区域。该方法不改变模型结构或显著增加计算负担。通过针对“护士”、“消防员”和“CEO”等概念的性别、种族和年龄偏见进行去偏实验。采用两名人工评估员手动检查1200张生成图像，并利用GPT4o进行自动偏见评估，对比其结果与人工评估的一致性。

Result: 人工评估结果表明，DeCoDi在缓解性别、种族和年龄偏见方面是有效的。GPT4o进行的自动偏见评估与人工评估结果没有显著统计学差异，且评估者之间具有高度一致性，同时覆盖了更广泛的受保护属性。

Conclusion: DeCoDi方法有望显著提高扩散模型生成图像的多样性，为文本到图像生成模型中的偏见问题提供了一个高效、易于实施且普适的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose DeCoDi, a debiasing procedure for text-to-image diffusion-based
models that changes the inference procedure, does not significantly change
image quality, has negligible compute overhead, and can be applied in any
diffusion-based image generation model. DeCoDi changes the diffusion process to
avoid latent dimension regions of biased concepts. While most deep learning
debiasing methods require complex or compute-intensive interventions, our
method is designed to change only the inference procedure. Therefore, it is
more accessible to a wide range of practitioners. We show the effectiveness of
the method by debiasing for gender, ethnicity, and age for the concepts of
nurse, firefighter, and CEO. Two distinct human evaluators manually inspect
1,200 generated images. Their evaluation results provide evidence that our
method is effective in mitigating biases based on gender, ethnicity, and age.
We also show that an automatic bias evaluation performed by the GPT4o is not
significantly statistically distinct from a human evaluation. Our evaluation
shows promising results, with reliable levels of agreement between evaluators
and more coverage of protected attributes. Our method has the potential to
significantly improve the diversity of images it generates by diffusion-based
text-to-image generative models.

</details>

### [240] [Privacy Preserving Inference of Personalized Content for Out of Matrix Users](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14905)
*Michael Sun,Tai Vu,Andrew Wang*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: DeepNaniNet是一个深度神经网络推荐框架，通过归纳图架构和BERT嵌入解决利基和动态社区中数据稀疏、冷启动和隐私挑战，并在多个基准测试中取得先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利基和动态社区的推荐系统面临数据稀疏、用户/物品冷启动以及隐私限制等挑战。传统方法在这种环境下表现不佳，或需侵入性用户数据，或在缺乏偏好历史时失效。

Method: 本文提出了DeepNaniNet，一个深度神经网络推荐框架，采用归纳图架构结合用户-物品交互、物品-物品关系和BERT衍生的文本评论嵌入。它通过新颖的“内容篮子”用户表示和基于自编码器的泛化策略实现无用户画像挖掘的冷启动推荐。同时引入了AnimeULike数据集用于评估。

Result: DeepNaniNet在CiteULike基准测试中取得了最先进的冷启动结果；在用户召回方面与DropoutNet相当，且对矩阵外用户无性能下降；在AnimeULike暖启动中，Recall@100分别比Weighted Matrix Factorization (WMF)高出7倍，比DropoutNet高出1.5倍。

Conclusion: DeepNaniNet能够在数据稀疏、冷启动严重的环境中提供高质量、保护隐私的推荐，同时有效整合异构内容源。

Abstract: Recommender systems for niche and dynamic communities face persistent
challenges from data sparsity, cold start users and items, and privacy
constraints. Traditional collaborative filtering and content-based approaches
underperform in these settings, either requiring invasive user data or failing
when preference histories are absent. We present DeepNaniNet, a deep neural
recommendation framework that addresses these challenges through an inductive
graph-based architecture combining user-item interactions, item-item relations,
and rich textual review embeddings derived from BERT. Our design enables cold
start recommendations without profile mining, using a novel "content basket"
user representation and an autoencoder-based generalization strategy for unseen
users. We introduce AnimeULike, a new dataset of 10,000 anime titles and 13,000
users, to evaluate performance in realistic scenarios with high proportions of
guest or low-activity users. DeepNaniNet achieves state-of-the-art cold start
results on the CiteULike benchmark, matches DropoutNet in user recall without
performance degradation for out-of-matrix users, and outperforms Weighted
Matrix Factorization (WMF) and DropoutNet on AnimeULike warm start by up to 7x
and 1.5x in Recall@100, respectively. Our findings demonstrate that DeepNaniNet
delivers high-quality, privacy-preserving recommendations in data-sparse, cold
start-heavy environments while effectively integrating heterogeneous content
sources.

</details>


### [241] [Collaborative Filtering using Variational Quantum Hopfield Associative Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14906)
*Amir Kermanshahani,Ebrahim Ardeshir-Larijani,Rakesh Saini,Saif Al-Kuwari*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合量子霍普菲尔德联想记忆 (QHAM) 和深度神经网络的混合推荐系统，在MovieLens 1M数据集上实现了高效的数据提取和分类。即使在模拟噪声环境下，系统也展现出稳定的高性能，并且优化了量子比特开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用量子计算在数据处理和模式识别方面的优势，尤其是量子机器学习 (QML) 的强大工具，以改进推荐系统的数据提取和分类能力，并处理真实世界数据集（如MovieLens 1M）。

Method: 研究者提出了一种混合推荐系统，该系统融合了量子霍普菲尔德联想记忆 (QHAM) 和深度神经网络。首先，使用 K-Means 算法将用户原型聚类成组，并通过编码器的激活函数转换为极性模式。随后，这些极性模式被整合到基于变分 QHAM 的混合推荐模型中。此外，通过仅高效更新一个随机目标量子比特，优化了此前 QHAM 架构中的量子比特开销。

Result: 在理想环境下，经过35个 epoch 训练，系统获得了 0.9795 的 ROC 值、0.8841 的准确率和 0.8786 的 F-1 Score。在模拟噪声环境下，系统取得了 0.9177 的 ROC 值、0.8013 的准确率和 0.7866 的 F-1 Score，显示出一致的性能。同时，该研究成功优化了 QHAM 架构中的量子比特开销。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个结合变分量子计算和深度学习的新颖框架，能够有效处理真实世界数据集，并展现出与纯经典方法相当的性能。模型在噪声配置下表现稳定，为未来推荐系统的发展提供了有前景的方向。

Abstract: Quantum computing, with its ability to do exponentially faster computation
compared to classical systems, has found novel applications in various fields
such as machine learning and recommendation systems. Quantum Machine Learning
(QML), which integrates quantum computing with machine learning techniques,
presents powerful new tools for data processing and pattern recognition. This
paper proposes a hybrid recommendation system that combines Quantum Hopfield
Associative Memory (QHAM) with deep neural networks to improve the extraction
and classification on the MovieLens 1M dataset. User archetypes are clustered
into multiple unique groups using the K-Means algorithm and converted into
polar patterns through the encoder's activation function. These polar patterns
are then integrated into the variational QHAM-based hybrid recommendation
model. The system was trained using the MSE loss over 35 epochs in an ideal
environment, achieving an ROC value of 0.9795, an accuracy of 0.8841, and an
F-1 Score of 0.8786. Trained with the same number of epochs in a noisy
environment using a custom Qiskit AER noise model incorporating bit-flip and
readout errors with the same probabilities as in real quantum hardware, it
achieves an ROC of 0.9177, an accuracy of 0.8013, and an F-1 Score equal to
0.7866, demonstrating consistent performance.
  Additionally, we were able to optimize the qubit overhead present in previous
QHAM architectures by efficiently updating only one random targeted qubit. This
research presents a novel framework that combines variational quantum computing
with deep learning, capable of dealing with real-world datasets with comparable
performance compared to purely classical counterparts. Additionally, the model
can perform similarly well in noisy configurations, showcasing a steady
performance and proposing a promising direction for future usage in
recommendation systems.

</details>


### [242] [Adversarial Attacks against Neural Ranking Models via In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15283)
*Amin Bigdeli,Negar Arabzadeh,Ebrahim Bagheri,Charles L. A. Clarke*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出Few-Shot Adversarial Prompting (FSAP)，一种利用大型语言模型(LLM)的语境学习能力，通过少样本提示生成高排名、语法流畅且具有误导性内容的对抗性文档的黑盒攻击框架，对神经排序模型构成严重威胁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经排序模型(NRMs)虽高效，但易受对抗性操纵。现有攻击方法依赖于词元级扰动或手动重写，且通常需要梯度访问。本研究旨在开发一种无需梯度访问或内部模型干预的黑盒攻击框架，能够生成自然且具有误导性的对抗性文档。

Method: FSAP框架利用LLM的语境学习能力，通过少样本提示来生成对抗性文档。它不需要梯度访问或内部模型工具。通过在少量有害示例的支持集上对LLM进行条件化，FSAP能合成语法流畅、主题连贯且巧妙嵌入错误信息的文档。FSAP有两种模式：FSAP-IntraQ（利用相同查询的有害示例增强主题保真度）和FSAP-InterQ（通过无关查询间的模式转移实现更广泛的泛化）。

Result: 在TREC 2020和2021健康错误信息轨迹上，针对四种神经排序模型的实验表明，FSAP生成的文档始终优于可信、事实准确的文档。此外，这些对抗性输出表现出强大的立场一致性和低可检测性，对神经检索系统构成现实且可扩展的威胁。FSAP还能有效泛化到专有和开源LLM。

Conclusion: FSAP是一种有效且可扩展的黑盒对抗性攻击框架，它利用LLM的语境学习能力生成具有欺骗性和高排名的错误信息文档，对神经检索系统构成了重大且可信的威胁。

Abstract: While neural ranking models (NRMs) have shown high effectiveness, they remain
susceptible to adversarial manipulation. In this work, we introduce Few-Shot
Adversarial Prompting (FSAP), a novel black-box attack framework that leverages
the in-context learning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) to
generate high-ranking adversarial documents. Unlike previous approaches that
rely on token-level perturbations or manual rewriting of existing documents,
FSAP formulates adversarial attacks entirely through few-shot prompting,
requiring no gradient access or internal model instrumentation. By conditioning
the LLM on a small support set of previously observed harmful examples, FSAP
synthesizes grammatically fluent and topically coherent documents that subtly
embed false or misleading information and rank competitively against authentic
content. We instantiate FSAP in two modes: FSAP-IntraQ, which leverages harmful
examples from the same query to enhance topic fidelity, and FSAP-InterQ, which
enables broader generalization by transferring adversarial patterns across
unrelated queries. Our experiments on the TREC 2020 and 2021 Health
Misinformation Tracks, using four diverse neural ranking models, reveal that
FSAP-generated documents consistently outrank credible, factually accurate
documents. Furthermore, our analysis demonstrates that these adversarial
outputs exhibit strong stance alignment and low detectability, posing a
realistic and scalable threat to neural retrieval systems. FSAP also
effectively generalizes across both proprietary and open-source LLMs.

</details>

### [243] [Retrieval-Augmented Review Generation for Poisoning Recommender Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15252)
*Shiyi Yang,Xinshu Li,Guanglin Zhou,Chen Wang,Xiwei Xu,Liming Zhu,Lina Yao*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出RAGAN框架，利用多模态基础模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力，生成高质量虚假用户画像及评论，以对黑盒推荐系统进行数据投毒攻击，实现了最先进的攻击性能，并揭示了推荐系统的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐系统极易受到数据投毒攻击，攻击者需在有限知识下生成可迁移且不可察觉的虚假用户画像。然而，受限于资源，生成高质量画像具有挑战性，且现有虚假文本评论质量差，严重损害了攻击效果和隐蔽性。

Method: 本文提出RAGAN框架，通过利用多模态基础模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力来增强评论文本质量。具体而言，引入了演示检索算法和文本风格迁移策略来增强朴素ICL。RAGAN框架由一个“越狱器”生成画像，并由一个“指导代理”和一个“守护者”协同优化，以提高攻击的可迁移性和不可察觉性。

Result: 在各种真实世界数据集上进行的综合实验表明，RAGAN实现了最先进（state-of-the-art）的数据投毒攻击性能。

Conclusion: RAGAN框架能够生成高质量的虚假用户画像，有效实施投毒攻击，并为理解推荐系统的鲁棒性提供了深刻见解。

Abstract: Recent studies have shown that recommender systems (RSs) are highly
vulnerable to data poisoning attacks, where malicious actors inject fake user
profiles, including a group of well-designed fake ratings, to manipulate
recommendations. Due to security and privacy constraints in practice, attackers
typically possess limited knowledge of the victim system and thus need to craft
profiles that have transferability across black-box RSs. To maximize the attack
impact, the profiles often remains imperceptible. However, generating such
high-quality profiles with the restricted resources is challenging. Some works
suggest incorporating fake textual reviews to strengthen the profiles; yet, the
poor quality of the reviews largely undermines the attack effectiveness and
imperceptibility under the practical setting.
  To tackle the above challenges, in this paper, we propose to enhance the
quality of the review text by harnessing in-context learning (ICL) capabilities
of multimodal foundation models. To this end, we introduce a demonstration
retrieval algorithm and a text style transfer strategy to augment the navie
ICL. Specifically, we propose a novel practical attack framework named RAGAN to
generate high-quality fake user profiles, which can gain insights into the
robustness of RSs. The profiles are generated by a jailbreaker and
collaboratively optimized on an instructional agent and a guardian to improve
the attack transferability and imperceptibility. Comprehensive experiments on
various real-world datasets demonstrate that RAGAN achieves the
state-of-the-art poisoning attack performance.

</details>


### [244] [A Systematic Survey of Model Extraction Attacks and Defenses: State-of-the-Art and Perspectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15031)
*Kaixiang Zhao,Lincan Li,Kaize Ding,Neil Zhenqiang Gong,Yue Zhao,Yushun Dong*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文对MLaaS平台上的模型提取攻击（MEAs）及其防御策略进行了全面综述，提出了新的分类法，并分析了攻击技术、防御挑战及其对人工智能安全和隐私的深远影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLaaS平台虽然提高了机器学习的可及性，但也引入了模型提取攻击（MEAs）的漏洞，威胁到知识产权、隐私和系统安全。因此，有必要对MEAs及其防御策略进行全面分析和理解。

Method: 本文通过对MEAs及其防御策略进行全面文献综述，提出了一种基于攻击机制、防御方法和计算环境的新型分类法。分析了各种攻击技术及其有效性，并评估了现有防御措施面临的挑战（特别是模型效用与安全之间的权衡）。此外，还探讨了MEAs在不同计算范式下的应用及其技术、伦理、法律和社会影响。

Result: 本文提供了一个关于MEAs及其防御策略的全面综述，并建立了一个新颖的分类体系。研究分析了各种攻击技术的效果，并识别出当前防御机制在模型效用和安全之间存在的关键权衡。同时，评估了MEAs在不同计算环境中的表现及其多方面影响。

Conclusion: 本系统性综述旨在为AI安全和隐私领域的专家提供宝贵参考，强调了MEAs领域面临的挑战和未来的研究方向，并维护了一个在线文献库以持续更新相关资料。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) models have significantly grown in complexity and
utility, driving advances across multiple domains. However, substantial
computational resources and specialized expertise have historically restricted
their wide adoption. Machine-Learning-as-a-Service (MLaaS) platforms have
addressed these barriers by providing scalable, convenient, and affordable
access to sophisticated ML models through user-friendly APIs. While this
accessibility promotes widespread use of advanced ML capabilities, it also
introduces vulnerabilities exploited through Model Extraction Attacks (MEAs).
Recent studies have demonstrated that adversaries can systematically replicate
a target model's functionality by interacting with publicly exposed interfaces,
posing threats to intellectual property, privacy, and system security. In this
paper, we offer a comprehensive survey of MEAs and corresponding defense
strategies. We propose a novel taxonomy that classifies MEAs according to
attack mechanisms, defense approaches, and computing environments. Our analysis
covers various attack techniques, evaluates their effectiveness, and highlights
challenges faced by existing defenses, particularly the critical trade-off
between preserving model utility and ensuring security. We further assess MEAs
within different computing paradigms and discuss their technical, ethical,
legal, and societal implications, along with promising directions for future
research. This systematic survey aims to serve as a valuable reference for
researchers, practitioners, and policymakers engaged in AI security and
privacy. Additionally, we maintain an online repository continuously updated
with related literature at https://github.com/kzhao5/ModelExtractionPapers.

</details>


### [245] [MoEcho: Exploiting Side-Channel Attacks to Compromise User Privacy in Mixture-of-Experts LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15036)
*Ruyi Ding,Tianhong Xu,Xinyi Shen,Aidong Adam Ding,Yunsi Fei*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了混合专家模型（MoE）中基于自适应路由的隐私侧信道攻击，提出了MoEcho框架和多种攻击方法，证明了其在LLMs和VLMs中推断和重建用户数据的能力，并呼吁立即采取防护措施。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer架构在AI领域取得巨大进展，其中MoE模型在效率和性能之间提供了良好平衡。然而，MoE模型的自适应路由（即输入依赖的专家激活模式）在硬件执行中留下独特的时空痕迹，这无意中为攻击者推断敏感用户数据打开了新的隐私泄露攻击面，亟需进行安全分析。

Method: 本研究提出了MoEcho框架，通过发现基于侧信道分析的攻击面来危害MoE系统的用户隐私。具体来说，MoEcho在不同计算平台（CPU上的缓存占用通道和Pageout+Reload，GPU上的性能计数器和TLB Evict+Reload）上引入了四种新颖的架构侧信道。利用这些漏洞，提出了四种攻击：提示推理攻击、响应重建攻击、视觉推理攻击和视觉重建攻击，以在基于MoE架构的大型语言模型（LLMs）和视觉语言模型（VLMs）中有效窃取用户隐私。

Result: MoEcho成功地发现了MoE架构中的侧信道分析攻击面，并基于此在CPU和GPU上引入了四种新颖的架构侧信道。利用这些漏洞，本研究提出的四种攻击（提示推理、响应重建、视觉推理、视觉重建）能够有效地在基于MoE的LLMs和VLMs中窃取用户隐私。

Conclusion: MoEcho是首次对现代Transformer中流行的MoE结构进行运行时架构级别的安全分析，揭示了其严重的安全性与隐私威胁。这凸显了在开发高效大规模AI服务时，在利用MoE模型时需要采取有效和及时的防护措施。

Abstract: The transformer architecture has become a cornerstone of modern AI, fueling
remarkable progress across applications in natural language processing,
computer vision, and multimodal learning. As these models continue to scale
explosively for performance, implementation efficiency remains a critical
challenge. Mixture of Experts (MoE) architectures, selectively activating
specialized subnetworks (experts), offer a unique balance between model
accuracy and computational cost. However, the adaptive routing in MoE
architectures, where input tokens are dynamically directed to specialized
experts based on their semantic meaning inadvertently opens up a new attack
surface for privacy breaches. These input-dependent activation patterns leave
distinctive temporal and spatial traces in hardware execution, which
adversaries could exploit to deduce sensitive user data. In this work, we
propose MoEcho, discovering a side channel analysis based attack surface that
compromises user privacy on MoE based systems. Specifically, in MoEcho, we
introduce four novel architectural side channels on different computing
platforms, including Cache Occupancy Channels and Pageout+Reload on CPUs, and
Performance Counter and TLB Evict+Reload on GPUs, respectively. Exploiting
these vulnerabilities, we propose four attacks that effectively breach user
privacy in large language models (LLMs) and vision language models (VLMs) based
on MoE architectures: Prompt Inference Attack, Response Reconstruction Attack,
Visual Inference Attack, and Visual Reconstruction Attack. MoEcho is the first
runtime architecture level security analysis of the popular MoE structure
common in modern transformers, highlighting a serious security and privacy
threat and calling for effective and timely safeguards when harnessing MoE
based models for developing efficient large scale AI services.

</details>


### [246] [IPIGuard: A Novel Tool Dependency Graph-Based Defense Against Indirect Prompt Injection in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15310)
*Hengyu An,Jinghuai Zhang,Tianyu Du,Chunyi Zhou,Qingming Li,Tao Lin,Shouling Ji*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出IPIGuard防御范式，通过构建工具依赖图解耦规划与外部数据交互，有效抵御间接提示注入（IPI）攻击，提升LLM代理系统的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM代理在与不可信数据源交互时易受间接提示注入（IPI）攻击，现有防御方法依赖模型固有安全性，未能从根本上限制代理的工具调用，导致其仍易受高级攻击向量影响。

Method: 提出IPIGuard防御范式，将代理任务执行建模为规划的工具依赖图（TDG）遍历。通过明确解耦行动规划与外部数据交互，显著减少注入指令触发的意外工具调用。

Result: 在AgentDojo基准测试中，IPIGuard在有效性和鲁棒性之间取得了卓越平衡，显著增强了对IPI攻击的抵御能力。

Conclusion: IPIGuard为在动态环境中开发更安全的代理系统奠定了基础，通过结构性限制代理行为，解决了现有防御的根本弱点。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are widely deployed in real-world
applications, where they leverage tools to retrieve and manipulate external
data for complex tasks. However, when interacting with untrusted data sources
(e.g., fetching information from public websites), tool responses may contain
injected instructions that covertly influence agent behaviors and lead to
malicious outcomes, a threat referred to as Indirect Prompt Injection (IPI).
Existing defenses typically rely on advanced prompting strategies or auxiliary
detection models. While these methods have demonstrated some effectiveness,
they fundamentally rely on assumptions about the model's inherent security,
which lacks structural constraints on agent behaviors. As a result, agents
still retain unrestricted access to tool invocations, leaving them vulnerable
to stronger attack vectors that can bypass the security guardrails of the
model. To prevent malicious tool invocations at the source, we propose a novel
defensive task execution paradigm, called IPIGuard, which models the agents'
task execution process as a traversal over a planned Tool Dependency Graph
(TDG). By explicitly decoupling action planning from interaction with external
data, IPIGuard significantly reduces unintended tool invocations triggered by
injected instructions, thereby enhancing robustness against IPI attacks.
Experiments on the AgentDojo benchmark show that IPIGuard achieves a superior
balance between effectiveness and robustness, paving the way for the
development of safer agentic systems in dynamic environments.

</details>

dynamic, unstructured environments without reliance on centralized
communication or control. We validate our system through real-world

### [249] [AmbiSQL: Interactive Ambiguity Detection and Resolution for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15276)
*Zhongjun Ding,Yin Lin,Tianjing Zeng*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: AmbiSQL是一个交互式系统，通过自动检测和澄清Text-to-SQL中的查询歧义，显著提高了SQL生成的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM-based Text-to-SQL系统在翻译自然语言到SQL时易出错，主要障碍是查询歧义，这会导致用户意图被误解和SQL生成不准确。

Method: 开发了交互式系统AmbiSQL，该系统能自动检测查询歧义，并通过直观的多项选择题引导用户澄清意图。方法包括引入细粒度歧义分类法来识别影响数据库元素映射和LLM推理的歧义，并利用用户反馈重写歧义问题。

Result: 在歧义查询数据集上的评估显示，AmbiSQL在歧义检测方面达到了87.2%的精度。与Text-to-SQL系统集成后，SQL精确匹配准确率提高了50%。

Conclusion: AmbiSQL系统通过有效解决查询歧义，显著提升了Text-to-SQL系统的性能和实用性。

Abstract: Text-to-SQL systems translate natural language questions into SQL queries,
providing substantial value for non-expert users. While large language models
(LLMs) show promising results for this task, they remain error-prone. Query
ambiguity has been recognized as a major obstacle for LLM-based Text-to-SQL
systems, leading to misinterpretation of user intent and inaccurate SQL
generation. We demonstrate AmbiSQL, an interactive system that automatically
detects query ambiguities and guides users through intuitive multiple-choice
questions to clarify their intent. Our approach introduces a fine-grained
ambiguity taxonomy for identifying ambiguities that affect database element
mapping and LLM reasoning, then incorporates user feedback to rewrite ambiguous
questions. Evaluation on an ambiguous query dataset shows that AmbiSQL achieves
87.2% precision in ambiguity detection and improves SQL exact match accuracy by
50% when integrated with Text-to-SQL systems. Our demonstration showcases the
significant performance gains and highlights the system's practical usability.
Code repo and demonstration are available at:
https://github.com/JustinzjDing/AmbiSQL.

</details>

# q-bio.QM [[Back]](#toc)

### [250] [Fusing Structural Phenotypes with Functional Data for Early Prediction of Primary Angle Closure Glaucoma Progression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14922)
*Swati Sharma,Thanadet Chuangsuwanich,Royston K. Y. Tan,Shimna C. Prasad,Tin A. Tun,Shamira A. Perera,Martin L. Buist,Tin Aung,Monisha E. Nongpiur,Michaël J. A. Girard*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 整合视神经盘结构特征和视野功能参数可显著提高原发性闭角型青光眼（PACG）进展风险分类的准确性，其中下部视神经盘特征最具预测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在通过结合视神经盘（ONH）结构特征和基于扇区的视野（VF）功能参数的综合方法，对原发性闭角型青光眼（PACG）患者的眼睛进行慢速或快速青光眼进展分类。

Method: 纳入了随访时间超过5年且可靠视野检查次数超过5次的PACG患者。进展定义为：快速进展（VFI每年下降<-2.0%），慢速进展（VFI每年下降>-2.0%）。使用AI分割OCT体积以提取31个ONH参数。通过青光眼半视野测试定义每个半视野的5个区域，并结合这些区域的平均敏感度与结构参数来训练机器学习分类器（包括随机森林）。通过SHAP分析识别关键预测因子。主要结果衡量指标是利用结构和功能数据组合对慢速与快速进展者进行分类。

Result: 分析了来自299名患者的451只眼睛，其中369只眼睛进展缓慢，82只眼睛进展迅速。结合结构和功能特征的随机森林模型表现最佳（AUC = 0.87）。SHAP分析识别出六个关键预测因子：下部MRW、下部和下颞侧RNFL厚度、鼻颞侧LC曲率、上鼻侧VF敏感度以及下部RNFL和GCL+IPL厚度。仅使用结构或功能特征的模型表现较差（AUC分别为0.82和0.78）。

Conclusion: 结合视神经盘（ONH）结构和视野（VF）功能参数显著提高了原发性闭角型青光眼（PACG）进展风险分类的准确性。下部ONH特征，特别是MRW和RNFL厚度，最具预测性，突出了ONH形态在监测疾病进展中的关键作用。

Abstract: Purpose: To classify eyes as slow or fast glaucoma progressors in patients
with primary angle closure glaucoma (PACG) using an integrated approach
combining optic nerve head (ONH) structural features and sector-based visual
field (VF) functional parameters. Methods: PACG patients with >5 reliable VF
tests over >5 years were included. Progression was assessed in Zeiss Forum,
with baseline VF within six months of OCT. Fast progression was VFI decline
<-2.0% per year; slow progression >-2.0% per year. OCT volumes were
AI-segmented to extract 31 ONH parameters. The Glaucoma Hemifield Test defined
five regions per hemifield, aligned with RNFL distribution. Mean sensitivity
per region was combined with structural parameters to train ML classifiers.
Multiple models were tested, and SHAP identified key predictors. Main outcome
measures: Classification of slow versus fast progressors using combined
structural and functional data. Results: We analyzed 451 eyes from 299
patients. Mean VFI progression was -0.92% per year; 369 eyes progressed slowly
and 82 rapidly. The Random Forest model combining structural and functional
features achieved the best performance (AUC = 0.87, 2000 Monte Carlo
iterations). SHAP identified six key predictors: inferior MRW, inferior and
inferior-temporal RNFL thickness, nasal-temporal LC curvature, superior nasal
VF sensitivity, and inferior RNFL and GCL+IPL thickness. Models using only
structural or functional features performed worse with AUC of 0.82 and 0.78,
respectively. Conclusions: Combining ONH structural and VF functional
parameters significantly improves classification of progression risk in PACG.
Inferior ONH features, MRW and RNFL thickness, were the most predictive,
highlighting the critical role of ONH morphology in monitoring disease
progression.

</details>


### [251] [Can synthetic data reproduce real-world findings in epidemiology? A replication study using tree-based generative AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.14936)
*Jan Kapar,Kathrin Günther,Lori Ann Vallis,Klaus Berger,Nadine Binder,Hermann Brenner,Stefanie Castell,Beate Fischer,Volker Harth,Bernd Holleczek,Timm Intemann,Till Ittermann,André Karch,Thomas Keil,Lilian Krist,Berit Lange,Michael F. Leitzmann,Katharina Nimptsch,Nadia Obi,Iris Pigeot,Tobias Pischon,Tamara Schikowski,Börge Schmidt,Carsten Oliver Schmidt,Anja M. Sedlmair,Justine Tanoey,Harm Wienbergen,Andreas Wienke,Claudia Wigmann,Marvin N. Wright*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 本研究提出并使用对抗性随机森林（ARF）生成流行病学合成数据，成功复现了六项原始研究的关键发现，证明了ARF在流行病学数据合成中的有效性和可靠性，并指出降低维度能进一步提升数据质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成式AI合成数据方法在流行病学领域面临质量受限、计算需求高、非专业人士使用复杂以及评估策略无法直接反映统计效用等问题。一个未充分探索的关键问题是合成数据能否可靠地重现流行病学研究的关键发现。

Method: 本研究提出使用对抗性随机森林（ARF）作为一种高效便捷的表格流行病学数据合成方法。通过复制来自六项流行病学出版物（涉及血压、人体测量、心肌梗死、加速度计、孤独感和糖尿病等）的统计分析，并比较原始结果与合成结果来评估ARF的性能。此外，还通过限制数据集至相关变量来评估维度和变量复杂性对合成质量的影响。

Result: 所有重复的原始研究中，多个合成数据复本的结果均与原始发现一致。即使在样本量与维度比相对较低的数据集中，复现结果也与原始结果在描述性和推断性分析上高度匹配。降低维度和预先派生变量进一步提高了结果的质量和稳定性。

Conclusion: 对抗性随机森林（ARF）是一种有效且可靠的流行病学表格数据合成方法，能够成功复现原始研究的关键发现。该方法在不同数据复杂度和维度下均表现良好，且通过优化维度和变量，可以进一步提高合成数据的质量和稳定性，从而为流行病学研究提供可靠的合成数据解决方案。

Abstract: Generative artificial intelligence for synthetic data generation holds
substantial potential to address practical challenges in epidemiology. However,
many current methods suffer from limited quality, high computational demands,
and complexity for non-experts. Furthermore, common evaluation strategies for
synthetic data often fail to directly reflect statistical utility. Against this
background, a critical underexplored question is whether synthetic data can
reliably reproduce key findings from epidemiological research. We propose the
use of adversarial random forests (ARF) as an efficient and convenient method
for synthesizing tabular epidemiological data. To evaluate its performance, we
replicated statistical analyses from six epidemiological publications and
compared original with synthetic results. These publications cover blood
pressure, anthropometry, myocardial infarction, accelerometry, loneliness, and
diabetes, based on data from the German National Cohort (NAKO
Gesundheitsstudie), the Bremen STEMI Registry U45 Study, and the Guelph Family
Health Study. Additionally, we assessed the impact of dimensionality and
variable complexity on synthesis quality by limiting datasets to variables
relevant for individual analyses, including necessary derivations. Across all
replicated original studies, results from multiple synthetic data replications
consistently aligned with original findings. Even for datasets with relatively
low sample size-to-dimensionality ratios, the replication outcomes closely
matched the original results across various descriptive and inferential
analyses. Reducing dimensionality and pre-deriving variables further enhanced
both quality and stability of the results.

</details>
